<HEAD>
<TITLE>CERTIFICATION PURSUANT TO</TITLE>
<META NAME="author" CONTENT="Jeff &nbsp;Conrad">
<META NAME="date" CONTENT="03/30/2007">
</HEAD>
<BODY style="line-height:12pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=right><B>Exhibit 31.1</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B><BR></B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>CERTIFICATION PURSUANT TO</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>SECTION 302 OF THE SARBANES-OXLEY ACT OF 2002</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">I, Reza Zarif, certify that:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">1. &nbsp;&nbsp;I &nbsp;have &nbsp;reviewed &nbsp;this &nbsp;annual &nbsp;report &nbsp;of &nbsp;Probe Manufacturing, &nbsp;Inc.;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">2. &nbsp;&nbsp;Based on my knowledge, this report does not contain any untrue statement of</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a &nbsp;material &nbsp;fact &nbsp;or &nbsp;omit &nbsp;to state a material fact necessary to make the</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;statements &nbsp;made, in light of the circumstances under which such statements</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;were &nbsp;made, &nbsp;not &nbsp;misleading &nbsp;with &nbsp;respect &nbsp;to &nbsp;the period covered by this</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;report;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">3. &nbsp;&nbsp;Based on &nbsp;my &nbsp;knowledge, &nbsp;the &nbsp;financial &nbsp;statements, &nbsp;and &nbsp;other financial</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;information &nbsp;included &nbsp;in &nbsp;this &nbsp;report, &nbsp;fairly &nbsp;present &nbsp;in &nbsp;all material</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;respects &nbsp;the &nbsp;financial condition, results of operations and cash flows of</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the &nbsp;registrant &nbsp;as &nbsp;of, &nbsp;and &nbsp;for, &nbsp;the &nbsp;periods presented in this report;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">4. &nbsp;&nbsp;The registrant's &nbsp;other &nbsp;certifying &nbsp;officer(s) &nbsp;and &nbsp;I are responsible for</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;establishing and maintaining disclosure controls and procedures (as defined</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;in Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(e) and 15d-15(e)) for the registrant and have:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a) &nbsp;&nbsp;designed &nbsp;such &nbsp;disclosure &nbsp;controls &nbsp;and &nbsp;procedures, &nbsp;or caused such</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;disclosure &nbsp;controls &nbsp;and &nbsp;procedures &nbsp;to &nbsp;be &nbsp;designed &nbsp;under &nbsp;our</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;supervision, &nbsp;to &nbsp;ensure &nbsp;that &nbsp;material &nbsp;information &nbsp;relating to the</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;registrant, &nbsp;including its consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;us &nbsp;by others within those entities, particularly during the period in</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;which &nbsp;this &nbsp;report &nbsp;is &nbsp;being &nbsp;prepared;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b) &nbsp;&nbsp;evaluated &nbsp;the &nbsp;effectiveness &nbsp;of &nbsp;the &nbsp;registrant's &nbsp;disclosure</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;controls &nbsp;and &nbsp;procedures and presented in this report our conclusions</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;about &nbsp;the effectiveness of the disclosure controls and procedures, as</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of &nbsp;the &nbsp;end &nbsp;of &nbsp;the &nbsp;period &nbsp;covered &nbsp;by &nbsp;this &nbsp;report based on such</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;evaluation; &nbsp;and</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;c) &nbsp;&nbsp;disclosed &nbsp;in &nbsp;this &nbsp;report &nbsp;any &nbsp;change &nbsp;in the registrant's internal</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;control over financial reporting that occurred during the registrant's</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;most &nbsp;recent fiscal quarter (the registrant's fourth fiscal quarter in</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the &nbsp;case &nbsp;of &nbsp;an &nbsp;annual &nbsp;report) that has materially affected, or is</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;reasonably &nbsp;likely &nbsp;to &nbsp;materially &nbsp;affect, &nbsp;the registrant's internal</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;control &nbsp;over &nbsp;financial &nbsp;reporting; &nbsp;and</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">5. &nbsp;&nbsp;The registrant's other certifying officer(s) and I have disclosed, based on</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;our most recent evaluation of internal control over financial reporting, to</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the registrant's auditors and the audit committee of the registrant's board</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of &nbsp;directors &nbsp;(or &nbsp;persons &nbsp;performing &nbsp;the &nbsp;equivalent &nbsp;functions):</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a) &nbsp;&nbsp;all significant &nbsp;deficiencies &nbsp;and &nbsp;material &nbsp;weaknesses &nbsp;in &nbsp;the</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;design or operation of internal control over financial reporting which</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;are &nbsp;reasonably likely to adversely affect the registrant's ability to</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;record, &nbsp;process, &nbsp;summarize &nbsp;and &nbsp;report &nbsp;financial &nbsp;information; and</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b) &nbsp;&nbsp;any fraud, &nbsp;whether &nbsp;or &nbsp;not &nbsp;material, &nbsp;that &nbsp;involves &nbsp;management or</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;other &nbsp;employees &nbsp;who &nbsp;have &nbsp;a &nbsp;significant &nbsp;role &nbsp;in the registrant's</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;internal &nbsp;control &nbsp;over &nbsp;financial &nbsp;reporting.</P>

<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Director</P>

<HEAD>
<TITLE>CERTIFICATION PURSUANT TO</TITLE>
<META NAME="author" CONTENT="Jeff &nbsp;Conrad">
<META NAME="date" CONTENT="03/30/2007">
</HEAD>
<BODY style="line-height:12pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=right><B>Exhibit 31.2</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B><BR></B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>CERTIFICATION PURSUANT TO</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>SECTION 302 OF THE SARBANES-OXLEY ACT OF 2002</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">I, John Bennett, certify that:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">1. &nbsp;&nbsp;I have reviewed this annual report of Probe Manufacturing, Inc.;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">2. &nbsp;&nbsp;Based on my knowledge, this report does not contain any untrue statement of</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a &nbsp;material &nbsp;fact &nbsp;or &nbsp;omit &nbsp;to state a material fact necessary to make the</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;statements &nbsp;made, in light of the circumstances under which such statements</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;were &nbsp;made, &nbsp;not &nbsp;misleading &nbsp;with &nbsp;respect &nbsp;to &nbsp;the period covered by this</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;report;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">3. &nbsp;&nbsp;Based on &nbsp;my &nbsp;knowledge, &nbsp;the &nbsp;financial &nbsp;statements, &nbsp;and &nbsp;other financial</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;information &nbsp;included &nbsp;in &nbsp;this &nbsp;report, &nbsp;fairly &nbsp;present &nbsp;in &nbsp;all material</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;respects &nbsp;the &nbsp;financial condition, results of operations and cash flows of</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the &nbsp;registrant &nbsp;as &nbsp;of, &nbsp;and &nbsp;for, &nbsp;the &nbsp;periods presented in this report;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">4. &nbsp;&nbsp;The registrant's &nbsp;other &nbsp;certifying &nbsp;officer(s) &nbsp;and &nbsp;I are responsible for</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;establishing and maintaining disclosure controls and procedures (as defined</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;in Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(e) and 15d-15(e)) for the registrant and have:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a) &nbsp;&nbsp;designed &nbsp;such &nbsp;disclosure &nbsp;controls &nbsp;and &nbsp;procedures, &nbsp;or caused such</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;disclosure &nbsp;controls &nbsp;and &nbsp;procedures &nbsp;to &nbsp;be &nbsp;designed &nbsp;under &nbsp;our</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;supervision, &nbsp;to &nbsp;ensure &nbsp;that &nbsp;material &nbsp;information &nbsp;relating to the</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;registrant, &nbsp;including its consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;us &nbsp;by others within those entities, particularly during the period in</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;which &nbsp;this &nbsp;report &nbsp;is &nbsp;being &nbsp;prepared;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b) &nbsp;&nbsp;evaluated &nbsp;the &nbsp;effectiveness &nbsp;of &nbsp;the &nbsp;registrant's &nbsp;disclosure</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;controls &nbsp;and &nbsp;procedures and presented in this report our conclusions</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;about &nbsp;the effectiveness of the disclosure controls and procedures, as</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of &nbsp;the &nbsp;end &nbsp;of &nbsp;the &nbsp;period &nbsp;covered &nbsp;by &nbsp;this &nbsp;report based on such</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;evaluation; &nbsp;and</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;c) &nbsp;&nbsp;disclosed &nbsp;in &nbsp;this &nbsp;report &nbsp;any &nbsp;change &nbsp;in the registrant's internal</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;control over financial reporting that occurred during the registrant's</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;most &nbsp;recent fiscal quarter (the registrant's fourth fiscal quarter in</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the &nbsp;case &nbsp;of &nbsp;an &nbsp;annual &nbsp;report) that has materially affected, or is</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;reasonably &nbsp;likely &nbsp;to &nbsp;materially &nbsp;affect, &nbsp;the registrant's internal</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;control &nbsp;over &nbsp;financial &nbsp;reporting; &nbsp;and</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">5. &nbsp;&nbsp;The registrant's other certifying officer(s) and I have disclosed, based on</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;our most recent evaluation of internal control over financial reporting, to</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the registrant's auditors and the audit committee of the registrant's board</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of &nbsp;directors &nbsp;(or &nbsp;persons &nbsp;performing &nbsp;the &nbsp;equivalent &nbsp;functions):</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a) &nbsp;&nbsp;all significant &nbsp;deficiencies &nbsp;and &nbsp;material &nbsp;weaknesses &nbsp;in &nbsp;the</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;design or operation of internal control over financial reporting which</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;are &nbsp;reasonably likely to adversely affect the registrant's ability to</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;record, &nbsp;process, &nbsp;summarize &nbsp;and &nbsp;report &nbsp;financial &nbsp;information; and</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b) &nbsp;&nbsp;any fraud, &nbsp;whether &nbsp;or &nbsp;not &nbsp;material, &nbsp;that &nbsp;involves &nbsp;management or</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;other &nbsp;employees &nbsp;who &nbsp;have &nbsp;a &nbsp;significant &nbsp;role &nbsp;in the registrant's</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;internal &nbsp;control &nbsp;over &nbsp;financial &nbsp;reporting.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">DATED &nbsp;this &nbsp;26th &nbsp;day &nbsp;of &nbsp;March 2007.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;/s/ &nbsp;John Bennett</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;-------------------------------</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;John Bennett</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Chief Financial Officer </P>

<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>CERTIFICATIONS PURSUANT TO</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>18 U.S.C. SECTION 1350,</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>AS ADOPTED PURSUANT TO</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>SECTION 906 OF THE SARBANES-OXLEY ACT OF 2002</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">Pursuant to section 906 of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002 (subsections (a) and</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">(b) of section 1350, chapter 63 of title 18, United States Code), each of the</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">undersigned officers of Probe Manufacturing, Inc., a Nevada corporation (the &quot;Company&quot;), does hereby certify, to such officer's knowledge, that:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">The Annual Report for the year ended December 31, 2006 (the &quot;Form 10-KSB&quot;) of</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">the Company fully complies with the requirements of Section 13(a) or 15(d) of</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, and the information contained in the Form</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">10-KSB fairly presents, in all material respects, the financial condition and</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">results of operations of the Company.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">Date: &nbsp;March 26, 2007</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:12pt">/s/ &nbsp;Reza Zarif</P>
